DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # --- System dependencies ---
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          python3.11 \
          python3.11-venv \
          python3.11-distutils \
          python3-pip \
          telnet \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # --- Install latest pip for python3.11 ---
  RUN python3.11 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # --- Miniconda install (optional, but recommended for env management) ---
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # --- Set conda to not auto-update or prompt for license ---
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  # --- Create and activate a conda env with Python 3.11 ---
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11 && \
      echo "conda activate node0" >> /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # --- Make sure conda activate works in non-interactive shells ---
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # --- Set workdir to project root ---
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # --- Copy source code into container ---
  COPY . /workspace
  # --- Activate conda, upgrade pip, install build tools, install Hatchling, then install project via pyproject.toml ---
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  # --- Expose commonly used port (adjust as needed) ---
  EXPOSE 49200
  # --- Default to bash shell in conda env ---
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # --- System dependencies ---
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # --- Install Miniconda for Python 3.11 and environment management ---
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  # --- Create and activate a conda env with Python 3.11 ---
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11 && \
      echo "conda activate node0" >> /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # --- Make sure conda activate works in non-interactive shells ---
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  # --- Activate conda, upgrade pip, install build tools, install Hatchling, then install project via pyproject.toml ---
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # --- System dependencies ---
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # --- Install Miniconda for Python 3.11 and environment management ---
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  # --- Use bash for all subsequent RUN commands ---
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # --- Ensure latest conda and Python 3.11 availability ---
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda info && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda search python=3.11
  # --- Create and activate a conda env with Python 3.11 ---
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11 && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda init bash && \
      echo "conda activate node0" >> /root/.bashrc
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  # --- Activate conda, upgrade pip, install build tools, install Hatchling, then install project via pyproject.toml ---
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # --- System dependencies ---

      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # --- Install Miniconda for Python 3.11 and environment management ---
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  # --- Use bash for all subsequent RUN commands ---
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # --- Create and activate a conda env with Python 3.11 ---
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11 && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda init bash && \
      echo "conda activate node0" >> /root/.bashrc
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  # --- Activate conda, upgrade pip, install build tools, install Hatchling, then install project via pyproject.toml ---
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # --- System dependencies ---
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # --- Install Miniconda for Python 3.11 and environment management ---
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  # --- Use bash for all subsequent RUN commands ---
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # --- Create the conda env with Python 3.11 ---
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  # --- Activate conda, upgrade pip, install build tools, install Hatchling, then install project via pyproject.toml ---
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # --- System dependencies ---
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # --- Install Miniconda for Python 3.11 and environment management ---
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  # --- Use bash for all subsequent RUN commands ---
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # --- Create the conda env with Python 3.11 ---
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  # --- Activate conda, upgrade pip, install build tools, install Hatchling, then install project via pyproject.toml ---
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  # --- System dependencies ---
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # --- Install Miniconda for Python 3.11 and environment management ---
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Verify conda installation
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda info
  # Ensure conda is properly initialized for bash
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda init bash
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  # --- Use bash for all subsequent RUN commands ---
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # --- Create the conda env with Python 3.11 ---
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  # --- Activate conda, upgrade pip, install build tools, install Hatchling, then install project via pyproject.toml ---
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda info
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda init bash
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Update conda itself before creating the environment
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y
  # Create the node0 environment with Python 3.11
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11
  # List environments for verification
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda env list && /opt/conda/bin/conda info --envs
  # Install pip in the node0 environment
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda install -n node0 pip -y
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \

          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \

      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda info
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda init bash
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda search python=3.11 -c conda-forge
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 -c conda-forge python=3.11
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda env list && /opt/conda/bin/conda info --envs
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda install -n node0 pip -y
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \

      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda info
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda init bash
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false \
      ACCEPT_CONDA_LICENSE=yes
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Removed problematic conda update step
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda search python=3.11 -c conda-forge
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 -c conda-forge python=3.11
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda env list && /opt/conda/bin/conda info --envs
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda install -n node0 pip -y
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda info
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda list
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update -n base conda -y && /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda env list && /opt/conda/bin/conda info --envs
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda install -n node0 pip -y
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  RUN source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install "hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e" && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge
  EXPOSE 49200
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda info
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda list
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update conda -y || true && /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda env list && /opt/conda/bin/conda info --envs
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda install -n node0 pip -y
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install 'hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e' && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge"
  EXPOSE 49200
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda search python
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11.4
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda env list && /opt/conda/bin/conda info --envs
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda install -n node0 pip -y

  COPY . /workspace
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \

      python -m pip cache purge"

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=en_US.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8 \
      PYTHONIOENCODING=UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          ca-certificates \
          locales \
          git \
          jq \
          wget \
          curl \
          lsof \
          rsync \
          build-essential \
          openssh-client \
          vim \
          netcat \
          && \
      locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && \
      update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8 && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda info
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda list
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda config --add channels conda-forge
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update conda -y || true && /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Removed: RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda update --all -y
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda init bash
  # Removed: RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda search python
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda create -y -n node0 python=3.11.4
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda env list && /opt/conda/bin/conda info --envs
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda install -n node0 pip -y
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && \
      conda activate node0 && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      pip install hatchling && \
      pip install 'hivemind @ git+https://github.com/learning-at-home/hivemind.git@4d5c41495be082490ea44cce4e9dd58f9926bb4e' && \
      pip install . && \
      python -m pip cache purge"
  EXPOSE 49200
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
